January 5 — 10:00 p.m. An observer in Bristol, Connecticut, sees about 13–15 large and dull lights in the sky. Some 10–12 of them are white and flying extremely fast in sync with each other, making swirly shapes. These lights disappear and reappear occasionally. Surrounding the white lights are three stationary black, dim lights in a triangular shape. The formation lasts more than 20 minutes, passes over the entire neighborhood, and is reminiscent of a light show. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 161498,” January 19, 2021; Rich Kirby, “ UFO Sightings in Connecticut: Here Are the Latest Reports,” Patch Media, Danbury, Conn., April 4, 2021)

January 6 — 5:45 p.m. A resident of Naugatuck, Connecticut, notices a bright, slightly bluish “ball of light with rope-like appendages hanging” from it. The sphere is followed a short time later by an exceptionally large and loud helicopter. (Rich Kirby, “UFO Sightings in Connecticut: Here Are the Latest Reports,” Patch Media, Danbury, Conn., April 4, 2021)

February 14 — Early morning. Scottish explorer Ashley Cowie photographs a ball of light that hovers above the rock formation known as the Temple of the Moon, an indigenous burial spot close to the summit of La Pena de Juaica, Colombia. More sightings follow, along with better quality images. In June, he obtains five clear photos of anomalous lights from his base at Palo Verde. The folklore of the local Muisca Indians refers to the Juaica lights as “glowing horsemen,” “golden balls,” “searchlights,” and “the charm.” In Muisca tradition, they are male and female spirits who combine as airborne lovers to produce rain. The earliest recorded mention of the phenomenon occurs in a Spanish document dating from 1606. (“ Project Juaica”; “ June 2021 UAP Report,” UAP Colombia, July 7, 2021; David Clarke, “Spooklights: A Survey of Transient Luminous Phenomena,” Fortean Times 422 (September 2022): 40)

February 21 — 12:19 p.m. An American Airlines Airbus A320 pilot reports a long, cylindrical object like a cruise missile pass above his location west of Clayton, New Mexico. The FAA has no reports of objects on air traffic controller radar screens. (“ Intercept: American Airlines Flight 2292 Reports Close Encounter with Unknown Flying Object,” Deep Black Horizon, February 21, 2021; Tyler Rogoway, “ FAA Releases Statement on Airliner’s Encounter with Unknown Object over New Mexico,” The Drive: The War Zone, February 24, 2021; John Greenewald, “ American Airlines Flight 2292 UFO Encounter, February 21, 2021,” The Black Vault, December 18, 2024)

March 24 — 7:30 p.m. A witness in Moosup, Connecticut, watches six fireballs that move “with intent and intelligence. Two of them appear to be floating; the one on the left moves from left to right and the other from top to bottom, while the other spheres stay in one place. The maneuvers continue for 5 minutes before it dissipates. (Rich Kirby, “ UFO Sightings in Connecticut: Here Are the Latest Reports,” Patch Media, Danbury, Conn., April 4, 2021)

June — Harjit Sajjan, the Canadian Minister of Defence, receives a briefing on Defence research, recent sightings, and historical information on UAP. (Tristin Hopper, “ First Reading: Canadian Military Suddenly Takes Notice of UFOs,” National Post (Canada), May 10, 2022; Keith Basterfield, “ The Canadian Government’s Interest in UAP between 2021 and 2024,” Unidentified Anomalous Phenomena—Scientific Research, May 16, 2024)

June 4 — According to Chen Li, a member of the Chinese Air Force’s Early Warning Academy in Wuhan, China, the Chinese armed forces have a task force on UAPs that uses artificial intelligence (AI) to analyze its data. Human analysts have been overwhelmed by increasing number of military and civilian sightings. The Chinese military uses a three-tier reporting system to gather and analyze UAP reports, and it assigns a “threat index” to each object “based on the observed behaviors, frequencies, aerodynamic design, radioactivity, possible make and materials,” and other pertinent information. A radar specialist is Xian says that the increasing use of drones is partially responsible for the increase in reports, as well as increased US military activities in he South China Sea. (Stephen Chen, “ China Military Uses AI to Track Rapidly Increasing UFOs,” South China Morning Post (Hong Kong), June 4, 2021; Tim McMillan and M. J. Banias, “ China Confirms It Has Its Own UFO Task Force,” The Debrief, June 4, 2021; Clark IV 1313, 1329)

June 7 — 2:32 p.m. The pilot of a Cessna C82R Skylane light aircraft observes a “25 foot long black triangular” object around 500 feet below them and to the right as they fly at around 6,000 feet near Los Angeles International Airport, California. The crew notifies the Los Angeles County Sheriff's Office. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Multiple UAPs Reported on FAA’s Internal Hotline in Just a Week,” The Drive: The War Zone, July 14, 2023)

June 12 — 5:10 p.m. The crew of an Envoy Air Embraer E170 airliner see a “white and diamond shaped” object traveling fast while they are flying southwest at around 20,000 feet and some 46 miles northeast of Palm Beach International Airport in Florida. The crew sees the UAP “pass underneath” them at around 19,500 feet. The “unknown phenomenon was smaller than their aircraft.” They notify the Palm Beach County Sheriff’s Office. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Multiple UAPs Reported on FAA’s Internal Hotline in Just a Week,” The Drive: The War Zone, July 14, 2023)

July 13 — 1:25 a.m. Ashley Cowie takes a long exposure photograph of a formation of flashing red lights moving in an arc beyond the ridge of the mountain La Pena de Juaica in Colombia. Another set of images taken in March 2022 shows a gaseous, shape-changing blob of light that takes on a vaguely anthropomorphic form. (David Clarke, “Spooklights: A Survey of Transient Luminous Phenomena,” Fortean Times 422 (September 2022): 40–41)

September 8 — A resident of Oxford, Connecticut, sees three bright but silent objects hovering for about 30–40 seconds right before an intense light appears that seems to be “scanning from front to back.” Something or someone is silently lowered out of one of the lights into a field across the street, then quickly drawn back up. Shortly afterward, the lights flash and disappear, but the witness can still see light trails left behind. (Rich Kirby, “ Are UFOs over Connecticut Growing Bolder? (We May Never Know),” Patch Media, Brookfield, Conn., January 1, 2022)

October — US diplomats in Bogota, Colombia, and Berlin, Germany, are being affected by Havana Syndrome. (“ Havana Syndrome: Berlin Police Probe Cases at US Embassy,” BBC News, October 9, 2021; “ Havana Syndrome Reported at US Embassy in Colombia,” BBC News, October 13, 2021)

Ufologist Jenny Randles identifies it as an Emirates Airbus 380 with the low sun illuminating its trail. (Jenny Randles, “Liverpool Echoes,” Fortean Times 413 (Christmas 2021): 29)

November 6 — 8.55 a.m. A witness in Marietta, Georgia, photographs a white, cigar-shaped object moving in a westerly direction. (“ Strange Cigar-Shaped Object Seen and Photographed,” UFOs Northwest, November 23, 2021)

November 11 — 5:13 a.m. A resident of Woodbury, Connecticut, sees a “bright orange glowing object” that resembles an “intense sunrise.” The fireball moves behind a hill and the sky returns to its normal nighttime color. (Rich Kirby, “ Are UFOs over Connecticut Growing Bolder? (We May Never Know),” Patch Media, Brookfield, Conn., January 1, 2022)

December 3 — 6:00 p.m. A woman driving in downtown Green Bay, Wisconsin, in foggy conditions, spots five lights moving in different directions. The lights merge into one. Three other oval, blue-purple lights also fly through the clouds. She then sees green lights moving very quickly. The sighting lasts 45 minutes and she takes several photos. (“ Groups of Multicolored Lights Move Rapidly on Foggy Night,” UFOs Northwest, December 4, 2021)

2022

An unnamed military platform in the US Africa Command takes a 31-second infrared video of a UAP. The footage shows an apparent heat signature with characteristics consistent with those of a physical object. However, AARO cannot determine whether the observed signature originates from a physical source, either as a thermal emission or a thermal reflection, or other source, such as a heat differential in the environment or sensor display error. The case is listed as insufficient information. (All-domain Anomaly Resolution Office, “ PR-001 Unresolved UAP Report, Africa 2022,” Defense Visual Information Distribution Service,” August 7, 2025)

January 31 — 11:00 a.m. An unnamed 93-year-old woman is walking along Robert Street in Milford Haven, Wales, when she sees a huge, round, shimmering object dipping in and out of the Milford Haven Waterway. It emits a cloud-like smoke from one side, then from the other side. Then the smoke shoots out of both sides simultaneously, going about 2 feet high. Then the object shoots off into the sky. (“ 93-year-old among First to Spot Possible UFO in Pembrokeshire,” Pembrokeshire Herald, February 4, 2022)

Early February — Night. Isabella Cooper is out for a walk with her father Justin on the Milford Haven side of the Cleddau Estuary. She takes a photo of a blue object several hundred feet in the air above the Valero Pembroke oil refinery. (“ Photographer Snaps Possible UFO Sighting in Pembrokeshire Skies,” Pembrokeshire Western Telegraph, February 8, 2022)

March 1 — The pilots of two F-35s observe a blue-green object while southbound at 36,000 feet near Glendale, Arizona. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Pilots Are Seeing Some Very Strange Things in Arizona’s Military Training Ranges,” The Drive: The War Zone, August 2, 2023)

April 22 — An F-345 pilot sees “8 silver UAS between 16,000 and 20,000 feet” in the vicinity of Glendale, Arizona. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Pilots Are Seeing Some Very Strange Things in Arizona’s Military Training Ranges,” The Drive: The War Zone, August 2, 2023)

April 22 — 8:52 p.m. The pilot of an Embraer Phenom business jet flying at 45,000 feet above Kessel, West Virginia, notices a light 10,000 feet above him. It changes to a string of lights. As he passes underneath, he notices the object’s lights go out and the aircraft’s avionics system fails. Other pilots can see the light as well. Probable Starlink satellite deployment. (John Greenewald, “ FAA Confirmed UFO Sighting April 22, 2022, by LXJ359 over Kessel, West Virginia,” The Black Vault, May 19, 2022; Groupe d’Études d’Information sur les Phénomènes Aérospatiaux Non-identifiés, “ Note d’enquête: Observations liées a Falcon 9,” July 4, 2022)

May 14 — A US military Reaper drone takes a 7-second video and six images of a cigar-shaped object north of Baghdad, Iraq, in an active combat zone. (John Greenewald, “ The ‘Baghdad Phantom UAP’ Imagery Published by Jeremy Corbell and George Knapp,” The Black Vault, March 7, 2023)

June 22 — 4:00 a.m. Philosophy instructor Carlos Paz Morales is driving north from Cafayate to Salta, Argentina, when a light comes flooding in through the rear window of his truck. He pulls onto the shoulder of the road near a rock formation known as El Sapo. He gets out and sees a large, white object in the hills not far away. It is cigar-shaped and moves from left to right in a zig-zag pattern. For the next 5 minutes he watches the object and takes some photos with his cellphone, then it vanishes in an instant. (“ Argentina: Teacher from Salta Claims Seeing UFO on the Way to Cafayate,” Inexplicata: The Journal of Hispanic Ufology, June 24, 2022)

July 6 — 5:06 p.m. A witness in Spruce Grove, Alberta, is followed by a black, triangular object that buzzes him then flies away. Later, pieces of what appears to be molten metal are found on the ground where he had been standing. (Chris Rutkowski, “ Some Interesting UFO Sightings Reported in 2022,” Ufology Research, February 6, 2023)

July 22 — 10:25 p.m. A married couple resting in their outdoor garden in Calangianus, Sardinia, Italy, notice a silent, illuminated object moving south to north above their house. It is oblong with sharp edges. The interior seems to have a sparkling light like a disco strobe. They see two luminous points on it that at first seem to flicker, but when they look at it through binoculars, the lights seem to be rotating. The object’s speed is constant and similar to that of an airliner. A photograph accompanies the report, but there is no mention of one being taken. (Stefano Innocenti, “ Ancora Ufo della Sardegna: Interessante Avvistamento nella Provincia di Sassari,” Il Faro (Fiumicino, Italy), July 30, 2022)

July 31 — Just before 12:00 midnight. A bizarre metal orb emblazoned with a secret code and perhaps containing “valuable information inside” falls from the sky onto a tree in Veracruz, Mexico, creating a firestorm of intrigue on social media and in local media. Meteorologist Isidro Cano Luna calls on the Mexican Navy to study the object. (Jason Koebler, “ Mysterious Metallic Orb Falls on Mexico, May Contain ‘Valuable Information,’ Meteorologist Says,” Vice, August 1, 2022)

August 3 — 10:45 a.m. A witness is driving down his driveway in a rural area of Oxford, Connecticut, when he sees a “bipedal creature about 4 feet tall” run out of the woods to his left, move across the driveway about 30 feet in front of him, and take off into the woods. The creature is brown, skinny, with no fur or hair, and looks like it is not even touching the ground. (Rich Kirby, “ Why Has There Been an Increase in UFO Sightings in CT?” Patch Media, Across Connecticut, January 2, 2023)

September 10 — 8:00 p.m. Witnesses sailing on the Fraser River near Vancouver, British Columbia, see a large, disc-shaped object, with a mirror-like finish on its underside, hovering above their sailboat. (Chris Rutkowski, “ Some Interesting UFO Sightings Reported in 2022,” Ufology Research, February 6, 2023)

October 7 — 10:30 p.m. An aircraft reports a UFO 5.7 miles south of La Crosse (Wis.) Regional Airport flying at 1,500 feet. The airport’s air traffic control also sees the object, which has alternating green, red, and blue lights and appears to “look like a jellyfish.” It is traveling westbound and shows up as a strong radar target. (John Greenewald, “ FAA Confirms ‘Jellyfish’-Like ‘Large Unknown Object’ over Minneapolis, Minnesota—October 7, 2022,” The Black Vault, December 20, 2022)

November 4 — Night. Pilots and flight attendants of Azul Flight 4248 see several lights moving quickly and changing colors over Lagoa dos Patos, Rio Grande do Sul, Brazil. The landing is delayed, and when the plane lands the pilot apologizes to the passengers, saying he had to report the sighting before landing. Carlos Fernando Jung of the Heller and Jung Space Observatory in Taquara, Rio Grande do Sul, finds an unidentified object near Lagoa dos Patos on photographic plates taken at the time. November 11 — 12:42 p.m. The pilot of a commercial airliner flying over Saint-Hyacinthe, Quebec, spots a drone flying uncomfortably close to his aircraft. The flight is at 9,000 feet and the crew watches as the drone flies within 200–300 feet off the left wingtip. (Chris Rutkowski, “ A Curious Collection of Canadian CADORS Cases,” Ufology Research, December 1, 2022)

December 9 — 9:40 p.m. A witness in Pottstown, Pennsylvania, sees a silent, triangle-shaped object with three dim orange lights moving slowly near the Limerick Generating Station on the Schuylkill River. The object heads south, then turns west at the plant. (“ Witness Report Claims UFO near Pennsylvania Nuclear Power Plant,” NorthCentralPA.com, January 27, 2023)

Goldwater Air Force Range in southwest Arizona sees a “small black, and metallic object” after detecting it on radar. 2023

An unnamed military platform in the US Africa Command takes a 4:58 infrared video of an apparent UAP. The footage shows an apparent heat signature with characteristics consistent with those of a physical object. However, AARO cannot determine whether the observed signature originates from a physical source, either as a thermal emission or a thermal reflection, or other source, such as a heat differential in the environment or sensor display error. The case is listed as insufficient information. (All-domain Anomaly Resolution Office, “ PR-003, Unresolved UAP Report, Africa 2023,” Defense Visual Information Distribution Service,” August 7, 2025)

January 5 — The pilot of a 56th Fighter Wing F-35 conducting a training sortie in the Gladden Military Operations Area in Arizona makes radar contact with a UFO at 18,700 feet. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Pilots Are Seeing Some Very Strange Things in Arizona’s Military Training Ranges,” The Drive: The War Zone, August 2, 2023)

January 19 — An F-16 Viper fighter jet flying in the Barry M. Goldwater Air Force Range in Arizona collides in mid-air with an “orange-white UAS.” The supposed drone strikes the fighter’s canopy. (Joseph Trevithick and Tyler Rogoway, “ Pilots Are Seeing Some Very Strange Things in Arizona’s Military Training Ranges,” The Drive: The War Zone, August 2, 2023)

January 29 — 11:15 p.m. A Canadian North air crew from Fort McMurray watches two unidentified yellow lights maneuvering east of the airfield at Yellowknife, Northwest Territories. The lights then shift to 10 nautical miles northwest of the city. The air traffic controller can see nothing and has no radar targets. (“ Canadian North Crew Reports ‘Lights in Sky’ over Yellowknife,” Cabin Radio, February 11, 2023; CADORS Report, no. 2023C0560, February 17, 2023)

February — Early morning. Pilots in two different aircraft observe a fast-moving, elongated white object in an undisclosed location in the US. The incident report states that the pilot “observed [the] unexplained phenomenon at my 2 o’clock at what appeared to be near my altitude or above. I am not sure the distance. At first I thought it to be a reflection in my windscreen, but after moving my head around and point of view, the object stayed steady.” “The object appeared rectangular or oblong and milky white,” the pilot states. “My First Officer (FO) returned from the forward [lavatory] and observed the object moving briskly southbound with me after I asked him ‘what is that’. It moved at steady speed southbound and disappeared.” “I regret not taking a video, but was taken by what I was seeing,” the pilot adds about the fleeting encounter. Within minutes, the pilot receives radio communication from a nearby ARTCC asking “if anyone had seen the light or object.” “Another flight captained by a friend also witnessed the Unidentified Aerial Phenomena (UAP), along with numerous other aircraft,” the pilot writes. “I have never witnessed anything like it in almost 30 years of flying.” (Micah Hanks, “ Pilot UFO Sightings Collected by NASA Reveal Serious Safety Concerns over Objects in US Airspace,” The Debrief, August 29, 2023)

February 1 — 9:30 p.m. Clark Watson observes, from his hotel room in Wyong, New South Wales, a white, blinking light move in from the direction of the ocean. It is joined by a second light and both dart around in the sky and move over the town at a high speed. The lights come in over Tuggerah Lake at around 1,500 feet, then swoop as low as 200–300 feet and move directly above his hotel. He records their movements with a 3-minute mobile phone video, which shows several indistinct, flickering lights moving around in the sky. At one point, the two lights maneuver around a third, solid, unmoving white light before heading back the way they had come. About one hour later, Watson sees a huge triangle with dim lights on its corners move in from over the ocean. It hovers at 400 feet. (“ ‘Giant Triangle’: Aussie’s ‘Mind-Blowing’ UFO Encounter,” news.com.au, September 1, 2024)

February 12 — 4:00 a.m. At least three different commercial flights over Quebec report “seeing very strange lights in the sky, high above the flight paths” that are “moving in a rapid and irregular way.” A crew member on a cargo flight from Chicago to Luxembourg reports to air traffic controllers that “It looks like it’s more than one and sort of circling.” ( CADORS Report, no. 2023Q0623, February 21, 2023)

February 14 — 2:00 a.m. The Atlanta, Georgia, Air Traffic Control Center is notified by three commercial flights of targets detected by all three aircraft’s Traffic Alert and Collision Avoidance Systems (TCAS). The targets that are detected by two Southwest Airlines pilots and one Spirit Airlines pilot are reported between the southeast and southwest arrival corridors of Hartsfield-Jackson International Airport. There is no mention of any visual contact made by any of the pilots. The mysterious targets are “not able to be verified” by the Atlanta Air Route Traffic Control Center. (Dustin Slaughter, “ As Congress Introduces New UAP Reporting Legislation for Pilots, FAA Reports Continue to Detail Flight Safety Incidents Posed by UAP,” The UAP Register, February 10, 2024)

February 14 — An object is detected floating over southeast Romania at an altitude of 36,000 feet. The Romanian Air Force quickly scrambles two MiG 21 Lancer jets to the scene, but they are unable to find the object. Later, Moldova closes its airspace for more than three hours due to an “object similar to a weather balloon” detected near the Ukrainian border. (“ Moldava Briefly Closed Its Airspace, Raising Tensions in a Country Shaken by the War,” New York Times, February 14, 2023; James Felton, “ Romania Sends Jets to Deal with Mysterious Object Floating in Its Airspace,” IFLScience, February 15, 2023)

March 1 — Eamonn J. Ansbro of the Kingsland Observatory in Boyle, County Roscommon, Ireland, says the facility has recorded about 40 instances of “balls of light” in the vicinity of Lough Key since the year 2000. The observatory’s camera tracking system has recorded them numerous times, but the images are usually fuzzy. He speculates that this is “because we are dealing with a … new space-time situation within the objects as they are casting their light. The whole time dilation is different … that’s why we get the fuzzy images.” (“UFO Hotspot Ireland Identified As Astronomer Says 40 Incidents Reported at Observatory,” Galway (Ireland) Beo, February 28, 2023)

March 26 — After 11:00 p.m. Several residents of Castrop-Rauxel, North Rhine–Westphalia, Germany, observe a point of light against the clouds. A cellphone video taken of the phenomenon seems to show another sphere leaving a trail of light in the air and through the clouds. The duration of 3 hours hints at a searchlight, with the video an artifact of the camera. (Andreas Müller, “ Kurioses Lichterschauspiel am Himmel über Castrop-Rauxel,” grenzWissenschaft-aktuell.de, April 3, 2023)

April — Morning. A pilot flying an air carrier out of an undisclosed airfield in New York State encounters a dark-colored object potentially “as large as a small business-type jet aircraft” that is also detected on the radar of the nearest air traffic control center. “During climb out on departure,” a portion of the pilot’s report reads, “we encountered an unidentified flying object or phenomena of some sort,” which reportedly occurs between the MSLIN and STOMP FIX geographical positions. “The object was brought to our attention by ATC when they advised us of a primary radar target that was at our 9 o’clock position within a half-mile distance,” the pilot states in the report. “The close proximity of the traffic advisory raised our attention to the threat.” The pilot states that the object is observed close to the 8 o’clock position on the captain’s side of the aircraft flying at the same altitude of 25,000 feet above mean sea level at the time the first visual contact is made. The object or aircraft seems to maintain its track, moving to the 7 o’clock position relative to the reporter’s aircraft, at which time it is no longer deemed a potential threat. The object, which cannot be identified by the pilot, is described as potentially being some kind of large unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) or possibly “a single ship military fighter/trainer aircraft,” which the pilot judges to have been traveling at least 200 knots. (Micah Hanks, “ Pilot UFO Sightings Collected by NASA Reveal Serious Safety Concerns over Objects in US Airspace,” The Debrief, August 29, 2023)

April 17 — 4:30 a.m. Frontier Airlines flight FFT1164 notifies an Air Traffic Control Center near Fort Bragg, North Carolina, that two bright lights in their vicinity are turning on and off at an altitude of 35,000 feet. The ATC confirms two primary targets at that location as the tracks appear and disappear on the scope. Suddenly, the two targets reappear two miles south of the position before disappearing completely. The encounter lasts approximately 25 minutes. (Dustin Slaughter, “ As Congress Introduces New UAP Reporting Legislation for Pilots, FAA Reports Continue to Detail Flight Safety Incidents Posed by UAP,” The UAP Register, February 10, 2024)

April 26 — 9:00 a.m. A witness is driving east on Killam Drive near the Wheeler Boulevard overpass in Moncton, New Brunswick, when he sees a white object with two windows hovering about 500 feet above the Moncton Coliseum. It fades out of sight or into the clouds by the time he reaches Millennium Drive. He estimates it is 70 feet wide with extensions that might be wings. (Bob Spearing, “ MUFON Cases #130602 & 130105 a Stealth B-21 Raider?” Mutual UFO Network news, November 13, 2023)

May 20 — At least 18 flights are suspended at Gaziantep Oğuzeli International Airport in Gaziantep, Turkey, after a commercial aircraft reports an alleged UFO on its radar at 9,000 feet. Air traffic control is also said to have detected the target. Flights resume 12 hours later. (“ Report: Turkish Airport Suspends Flights for 12 Hours Following ‘UFO Sighting,’” New Straits Times (Malaysia), May 20, 2023)

May 22 — 9:30 a.m. After China Airlines Flight CI152 reports a suspected drone-like object about 1,000 feet above a runway at Taoyuan International Airport, Taiwan, the airport suspends takeoffs and landings for about 40 minutes. (“‘ Unidentified Flying Object’ Forces Closure of Taiwan Taoyuan Airport,” Taiwan News, May 22, 2023)

May 29 — 7:53 p.m. A Morningstar Aircraft is flying above Bay St. Louis, Mississippi, when the flight crew observes an object about 6 feet in height with a white dome and a red device underneath it. It is less than half a mile from the airplane. (Chris Rutkowski, “ Mining the Transport Canada Incident Reports for UFOs,” Ufology Research, July 25, 2023)

June 3 — 10:00 a.m. Four witnesses in a parking lot across from the Meijer’s grocery store in Bad Axe, Michigan, hear a loud noise and see two military airplanes flying together. They appear to be interested in a white, metallic disc that overtakes the jets, hovers, spins, and outmaneuvers them. The jets apparently shoot some type of flares at it. The witnesses describe the maneuvers as a dogfight. After three attempts, the jets move away. The disc silently shoots off in the opposite direction. (“ Fighter Jets Circle UAP in Michigan on June 3,” National UFO Reporting Center, June 6, 2023; Mark Birdsall, “ Something Happened in the Skies over Bad Axe on June 3—But What?” Huron (Mich.) Daily Tribune, June 16, 2023)

June 27 — 7:50 p.m. Seven mystery drones fly above the Koh Nhek district, Mondulkuri province, Cambodia, appearing as fuzzy white lights in videos shot by local troops. The same type of drone was seen one week earlier. The Cambodian Border Troops initially think they are of Vietnamese origin, but the Vietnam government denies any involvement. Cambodian Prime Minister Hun Sen orders a detachment of 500 troops equipped with 200 anti-aircraft weapons to the border and offers a $20,000 bounty to any military unit that shoots one down. (“ Video: Unidentified Drones Spotted Flying over Cambodian Territory,” Khmer Times (Phnom Penh), June 28, 2023; “ PM Promises $20,000 Bounty for Military Unit Who Shoot Down ‘Mystery Drones,’” Khmer Times (Phnom Penh), June 28, 2023)

July 11–August — Villagers in the indigenous Ikitu village of San Antonio de Pintujacu, in the Alto Nanay district of Peru, claim that 7-foot-tall green entities with large heads and yellowish eyes are attacking them each night, causing injuries. They are impervious to bullets and move by floating. Representatives from the police and Peruvian Navy visit the area to assess the situation. (Sam Allcock, “ Peruvian Villagers Report Attacks by 7ft Armoured Aliens Resembling Green Goblin from Spider-Man,” Z News Service, August 7, 2023; “Peru vs. Aliens,” Fortean Times 436 (October 2023): 4–5; “ Peruvian Alien Encounter of June 2023,” Fiction, 2024)

July 14 — Australian astro-photographer Ari Rex captures an odd oblong light on a time-lapse image near Gundaroo, New South Wales. However, he later determines that “the mysterious object is actually the fumes from the Chandrayaan-3 rocket launched by India to explore the Moon.” (Georgia Curry, “ Canberra Astro-Photographer Captures Incredible Image in Our Night Sky,” Canberra Weekly, August 2, 2023; James Coleman, “ Canberra Astro-Photographer ’99.99% Sure’ UFO Mystery Is Solved,” Riotact, August 8, 2023)

July 28 — Portuguese MEP Francisco Guerreiro poses a question in the European Parliament on whether the European Commission, the European Defence Agency, or the European Union Aviation Safety Agency have any protocols for collecting UAP reports. (“ European Reports and Protocols on Unidentified Anomalous Phenomena,” European Parliament, Parliamentary Question E-002375/2023, July 28, 2023)

September 3 — 9:00 p.m. A woman is walking her dog a few blocks from the Susquehanna River in Cumberland County, Pennsylvania. Her dog, which is deaf, looks up into the sky and she sees a bright flash of light similar to a starburst. Hovering about 300 feet above her building is a massive, solid black, triangular object with rounded corners. The surface of the object has a flat-matte black color. It has no individual lights, but it has two circular protuberances on the back section that are possible vents, which have an orange color that she assumes is metal cooling down from an intense heat. Other indentations or protrusions are visible on the underside. She detects a barely audible humming sound, then a click as the object begins to move slowly away. Suddenly it takes off in a blur of speed and disappears. (Stan Gordon, “ Solid Black Triangular UFO/UAP Hovers Low over Pennsylvania Building,” Stan Gordon’s UFO Anomalies Zone, October 9, 2023)

October 13 — Evening. Residents and tourists on the beach at Mazagón, Huelva, Spain, watch and take videos of lights in the sky moving at impossible angles and high speed and changing colors. (“ Un avistamiento de un OVNI en la playa de Mazagón,” Huelva Información, October 15, 2023; Ulrich Magin, “And the Depths Below!” Fortean Times 440 (January 2024): 19)

November 18 — 11:02 a.m. Omni Air International Flight 1169 en route from Honolulu, Hawaii, to Fort Worth, Texas, encounters “several bright, erratic lights directly in front and above their flight path” as it approaches Los Angeles International Airport in California. Concerned about a possible collision, Flight 1169 requests “deviations 20 degrees left to avoid the lights.” Once granted by Air Traffic Control, the plane shifts course and then continues on its way without further incident. The flight returns to its original course, noting that the lights are “80 miles off their right side” and approximately over the El Toro FAA radio station, east of Costa Mesa, California. The FAA entry emphasizes that it is “not a UAS [unmanned aerial system] report.” (Dustin Slaughter, “ As Congress Introduces New UAP Reporting Legislation for Pilots, FAA Reports Continue to Detail Flight As Congress Introduces New UAP Reporting Legislation for Pilots, FAA Reports Continue to Detail Flight Safety Incidents Posed by UAP,” The UAP Register, February 10, 2024)

December 2 — 11:04 p.m. Air Traffic Control staff at Great Falls International Airport, Montana, spots more than five “lit objects flying in a circular pattern,” according to an FAA report. “Lights changed in intensity consistent with circling or holding pattern at different altitudes.” While some features of the sighting are consistent with a Starlink launch, additional details are not: “Movement not always circular in pattern, but at times appeared to form up in formation or move to/from the area.” Security personnel at Malmstrom Air Force Base, located 20 miles east, also witness the objects. (Dustin Slaughter, “ As Congress Introduces New UAP Reporting Legislation for Pilots, FAA Reports Continue to Detail Flight Safety Incidents Posed by UAP,” The UAP Register, February 10, 2024)

2024

An unnamed military platform in the US Africa Command takes a 1:18 infrared video of an apparent group of unidentified objects. AARO determines that the objects are almost certainly a group of migratory birds. (All-domain Anomaly Resolution Office, “ PR-002, Resolved as Migratory Birds, Africa 2024,” Defense Visual Information Distribution Service,” August 7, 2025)

January 31 — Portuguese MEP Francisco Guerreiro poses a question in the European Parliament on why the preparatory work for an EU Space Law does not include a UAP reporting and monitoring system. (“ UAP Monitoring and Reporting in the EU Space Law,” European Parliament, Parliamentary Question E-000318/2024, January 31, 2024; Jochen Ickinger, “ UAP in the European Parliament, Part 2,” UAP Check, February 28, 2024)

February 9 — 12:23 a.m. The pilot of a Jazz Aviation Bombardier Challenger CL600 business jet flying above Black Rock Mountain, Alberta, notices three bright lights that “grow dimmer.” More lights appear and disappear for the next few minutes. Air traffic control reports no air traffic in the vicinity. (Chris Rutkowski, “ UFOs Reported through Transport Canada on March 18–19, 2024,” Ufology Research, March 19, 2024)

February 12 — An American Airlines pilot reports a high-speed object with a flashing orange light while flying between Boston, Massachusetts, and Harrisburg. Pennsylvania. An audio recording posted on YouTube allegedly documents the conversation between the unidentified pilot and air traffic control. (“ Pilot Spots UFO While Flying from Boston: ‘Bright Orangy Thing,’” Flight Simulator Fantasy – F.S.F. YouTube channel, February 16, 2024; Timothy Frudd, “ Audio: Pilot Spots UFO Mid-Flight: Report,” American Military News, February 28, 2024)

February 16 — 7:04 p.m. Two pilots flying an airliner at 36,000 feet near or off the coast of South Carolina watch a large, triangular object, “roughly the size of a football field,” moving at about 4,000 feet below them. The object has three white lights at its corners and a central red light at its rear, which blinks out after 30 seconds. Neither onboard radar for the Traffic Collision Avoidance System detects it. After about 3 minutes, the object appears to emit a static discharge and vanishes, leaving the pilots to wonder whether it had accelerated or merely gone dark. They capture a few photos of the object on a cellphone. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC Sighting 180940,” April 27, 2024)

February 27 — 3:20 a.m. Two witnesses in Pozzuoli, Campania, Italy, see three whitish lights flying at a high altitude. After a few seconds, one manages to film the lights briefly before they disappear. (“ UFO Sighting in Pozzuoli: Mysterious Lights in the Night Sky,” Il Mattino (Naples), April 5, 2024)

March 1 — Canada’s Chief Science Advisor Mona Nemer announces that the first report of the Sky Canada Project will be ready in late summer or early fall. The project, launched in the fall of 2022, has contacted counterparts in the US and France, while also collecting information from Canadian departments and agencies like the Department of National Defence, Transport Canada, the Canadian Space Agency, and the Royal Canadian Mounted Police. (Canada, “ Sky Canada Project”; “ Canadian Government’s Top Science Advisor Provides Update on Official UFO Study,” CTV News, March 1, 2024)

March 10 — Early morning. After receiving a report of a pulsating orange blob above Scotts Bottom Road east of Green River, Wyoming, MUFON State Director Richard W. Beckwith heads to an observation point with a video camera, a telephoto lens, and a tripod. The light sems to oscillate back and forth for about 40 minutes, and at one point a smaller white light seems to emerge from it, hover for a few minutes, then disappear. Beckwith captures the object and its movements on video. (“ City Attorney for Rock Springs Captures Video of ‘UFO’ near Green River,” Cowboy State Daily (Lander, Wyo.), March 11, 2024)

March 16 — 7:04 p.m. German astrophotographer Sebastian Voltmer is taking videos of the Moon with a smartphone attached to a telescope on the Spicherer Höhen, a historical landmark on the French side of the border just south of Saarbrücken, Germany. He captures a swiftly moving bright object flitting across the lunar terminator. The high speed is improbable for a satellite or spacecraft, and although it could be a meteor, the International Meteor Organization does not show a match with a known observation. The telescope’s focus range rules out an insect, and a high-flying bird is unlikely because the sun has already set. (“ Strange Lunar Observation!” spacemovie YouTube channel, March 16, 2024; Andreas Müller, “ Bekannter Astrofotograf filmt unidentifiziertes Objekt vor dem Mond,” grenzWissenschaft- aktuell.de, March 19, 2024)

March 25 — 2:30 p.m. Spirit Airlines NKS 3380 passenger Michelle Reyes spots a “flying cylinder” from her window as her plane is heading into LaGuardia Airport in New York City. One other passenger also notices the object. She takes a video that she posts on her Facebook page and alerts the Federal Aviation Administration by email. The object appears to be flying very fast and is only on five frames of the video. MUFON investigator Thomas Wertman estimates the object is at 2,500 feet and relatively close to the aircraft. However, Mick West thinks the object is moving slowly and is consistent in appearance with a balloon. (“ Caught on Camera: Possible UFO Reported over New York’s LaGuardia Airport: Banfield,” NewsNation YouTube channel, April 25, 2024; “ UFO Spotted over New York City? Here’s Is the Truth,” The Economic Times, April 25, 2024; Metabunk.org thread, “ Michelle Reyes, LaGuardia UFO from Plane Window,” April 2024; National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC Sighting 180939,” April 27, 2024)

March 28 — 9:20 a.m. Mike Pritchard and his 13-year-old son are traveling south on Colorado Highway 9 approaching Hoosier Pass when they see a strange metallic object hovering just above the tree line on the left. It is spherical but slightly flattened at top and bottom, and apparently between 9 to 30 feet in diameter. Snowbanks prevent Pritchard from pulling over, so he continues watching it for about 2 minutes while he drives. (Robert Powell, “ UAP Sighting by SCU Member, Mike Pritchard,” SCU Review 6, no. 1 (January 27, 2025): 13–15)

April 8 — 11:30 a.m. Two people are in Irwin, Pennsylvania, entering the exit ramp from US Highway 30 to travel on Interstate 76 when they notice a smooth, white, cylindrical object low above the “business district.” It is distinctly visible against a cloudy background and seems rounded on the front end and square on the back. As the object rises higher in the sky, it becomes a brighter white. The total viewing time is 5–10 seconds. (Stan Gordon, “ Two Daylight, Low Level UFO/UAP Sightings Reported above Populated Communities in Southwest Pennsylvania, April 2024,” Stan Gordon’s UFO Anomalies Zone, April 15, 2024)

April 9 — During a meeting of Japan’s House Committee on Security, Rep. Yoshiharu Asakawa raises a question about whether the government is utilizing a UAP tracking platform similar to the Gremlin System used by the US Army. Defense Minister Minoru Kihara replies that he will propose developing such a data collection system. Asakawa asks whether the Japanese military is capable of intercepting UAP over sensitive areas, citing a report of objects near Prime Minister Fumio Kishida’s residence and Yokosuka Air Force Base. Defense officials reply that they have that capability, but are unable to verify the report. (Baptiste Friscourt, “ Japanese Minister of Defense Says Responding to Unidentified Objects Is ‘Essential,’” Sentinel News Substack, April 9, 2024)

May 28 — Japanese lawmakers form a nonpartisan council (the “Parliamentary League for UAP Clarification from a Security Perspective”) of 16 members chaired by former Minister of Defense Yasukazu Hamada that will ask the government to set up an agency to investigate UAP sightings from the perspective of national security. Former Environment Minister Shinjirō Koizumi will serve as secretary-general. The group will hold its founding general meeting on June 6. (Japan UAP Study Team, “ UFO Parliamentary League Established,” X post, May 28, 2024; “ Japan Lawmakers to Create Group for Government Probes into UFOs,” Japan Times, May 28, 2024; “ In the Name of Security, Diet Group Planned to Study UFOs,” Asahi Shimbun (Tokyo), May 29, 2024; Keith Basterfield, “ The Japanese Government and UAP” Unidentified Anomalous Phenomena—Scientific Research, June 1, 2024)

June 3 — 6:00 p.m. Air Traffic Control personnel at Stewart International Airport near Newburgh, New York, observe a 50-foot-long object appear about 4 miles to the southwest. It remains hovering at 4,000 feet for 50 minutes before disappearing into the clouds. Airport radar is unable to detect the object. AARO conducts an investigation. (Dustin Slaughter, “ Large ‘Boomerang-Shaped’ Object spotted near New York Airport Remains Unidentified, Pentagon Says,” The UAP Register, December 26, 2024)

July 2 — 11:15 a.m. A man is driving south on US Highway 119 about one mile south of Smithfield, Pennsylvania, when his radio gets “staticky” and his car stalls out. He notices a large, black, cylindrical object, perhaps 30 feet long and about 300 feet overhead. There is a pale-green haze around one end of the object. It hovers for a few seconds then moves off behind some trees where it alternately hovers and moves east for a few seconds about one mile away. He gets out of his car to take a few pictures with this cellphone, but they only show a dark object with no detail. Another motorist has pulled over after experiencing car trouble and seeing the object. The batteries on both cars appear to be dead, but they start up again after about 30 minutes. (“ Two Vehicles Stall on Pennsylvania Highway As Cylindrical UFO Passes Low Overhead (July 2, 2024),” Stan Gordon’s UFO Anomalies Zone, September 8, 2024)

August 1 — 8:00–9:00 p.m. A woman is with her teenage son at Anthony Lakes in eastern Oregon. She sees a small amber light across the lake flickering and blinking on the western shoreline. It blinks on and off several times before turning off for good. At 10:30 p.m., as they are walking along a trail near their campground, they see a bright orange and red light approximately 350 feet away and near the northwest part of the lake. They shine their flashlights at it, and the light begins approaching them, growing larger, but then stops and hovers about 6 feet above the water. They wake up her uncle at the campground, and he gets up and watches the light as well. The teenager says that there are flames around the sphere that look like plasma. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 183117,” September 23, 2024)

September 17 — 2:30 p.m. A US military pilot code-named Troy21 flying a Beechcraft Super King Air 350C on a classified flight involving a Homeland Security drug interdiction mission at 20,000 feet over Kings County, California, reports a gray, cylindrical object passing directly underneath his wing and traveling eastward. The pilot estimates the object to be 10 feet below the aircraft and flying at Mach 2 speed in 2 minutes. He then tracks the object via onboard radar about 60 miles away. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 183084”; Ashleigh Banfield, “ Military Pilot’s Reported Encounter with UFO: ‘This Is Going to Sound Weird,’” NewsNation, February 20, 2025; Shane Galvin, “ US Air Force Pilot Reports Close Encounter with ‘Football-Sized’ UFO in Leaked Audio: ‘Right under My Wing,’” New York Post, February 20, 2025; “ UFO ‘Tic Tac’ Encounter Described by Plane Crew Member,” NewsNation, April 24, 2025; “ Tic-Tac UAP Buzzes Homeland Security Flight,” National UFO Reporting Center, April 30, 2025)

October 3 — Two witnesses in Seaside, Oregon, watch a silent, triangular object, about 40–50 feet long and flying at 100–150 feet in altitude, approaching their property from the south. Two steady bright lights are at two of the corners and pointing down. A larger third light is in the center and blinking every 2–3 seconds. It moves away to the north, apparently following US Highway 101. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 183328,” October 7, 2024)

November 1 — 9:20 p.m. A commercial aircraft that has just taken off from Salt Lake City (Utah) International Airport en route to Rogue Valley International–Medford Airport in Oregon levels off at 36,000 feet and notices a group of about 5 or 6 bright white lights circling one another. The lights increase in speed corresponding to the intensity of the light. At one point, they form a triangle and remain motionless. The pilot and crew watch them for 45–50 minutes. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 183840,” November 8, 2024)

November 18–December 2 — Night. From five to twelve unidentified large drones are reported swarming above several areas in Morris County, New Jersey, including the US Army’s Picatinny Arsenal, for 2 hours on November 18. The drone sightings are followed by appearances of military aircraft, a Blackhawk helicopter, and a New Jersey State Police helicopter. The sightings continue nightly, except for November 28. It is perhaps this incident that prompts the FBI to open an investigation into the mystery drones. The FBI opens a tip line, at first locally, then statewide, which records more than 5,000 drone sightings by December 18. Nancy Read, who lives on Ironia Road in Mendham, sees groups of drones—one stationary, the others “in and out of the tree line”—for long periods of time between 8:00 and 10:00 p.m. near the Randolph Regional Animal Shelter. Witness Mike Walsh estimates the largest drones are the size of a car. One night he is on a ridge near Black River Middle School in Chester, where he counts eight drones flying at once. He also sees multiple drones above Randolph’s Company 4 Firehouse on Dover-Chester Road. Walsh reports the drones to Mendham and Randolph police. The Ocean County (N.J.) Sheriff’s Office’s Drone Unit, armed with a flight radar tracker, sets up a mobile command center at Hiering Avenue and Ocean Terrace in Seaside Heights to search for mystery drones; their radar definitely tracks unmanned devices that are 3–4 feet long and fly at speeds up to 60 mph. On the other hand, many of the videos posted on social media, upon analysis, actually do show aircraft. (Wikipedia, “ 2024 United States drone sightings”; Howard Altman, “ Army Arsenal Seeking Info on Mysterious Drone Flights over Installation,” The War Zone, November 19, 2024; Adam Harding, “ FBI Joins Hunt for Answers behind Nightly Drone Sightings in New Jersey,” WNBC-TV, New York City, December 2, 2024; Tina Kelley, “ Mysterious Drone Night Flights Leave N.J. Residents on Edge,” NJ.com, December 2, 2024; Nick Caloway, “ Video Shows Drones Circling the Skies of New Jersey: Here’s What the FBI Is Doing about Them,” CBS New York, December 3, 2024; Morris County (N.J.) Prosecutor’s Office, “ Law Enforcement Advises Public How to Report Drones Activity,” December 3, 2024; Kyle Morel, “ Mysterious Drone Sightings Continue in Additional North Jersey Spots: Here’s Where,” North Jersey Media Group, December 4, 2024; “ Ocean County Sheriff’s Unit Tracking Drones: See How They Are Confirming Sightings,” Asbury Park (N.J.) Press, December 15, 2024; Department of Homeland Security, “ CTAB: NJ Drones,” December 18, 2024; “ Many Videos That Purport to Show Drones in New Jersey Likely Show Planes, Visual Analysis Finds,” New York Times, December 19, 2024; John Greenewald, “ DHS Briefing Details Select Drone Sightings in New Jersey, Highlights Potential Misidentifications among 5,000+ Reports,” The Black Vault, May 5, 2025; Howard Altman, “ What Were the New Jersey Drones? Former High-Ranking FAA Official Gives his Take,” The War Zone, August 21, 2025)

December 3–4 — Unidentified drones are observed over the USAF’s Ramstein Air Base near Ramstein- Miesenbach, Germany, as well as above locations belonging to the German arms manufacturer Rheinmetall and the chemicals group BASF. (“ Mögliche Spionagedrohnen fliegen über US-Militärbasis Ramstein,” Der Spiegel, December 13, 2024; “ Unidentified Drones Spotted over US Air Base in Germany, Report Says,” The Guardian (UK), December 13, 2024; Thomas Newdick, “ U.S. Air Force Confirms Drone Sightings over Ramstein Air Base in Germany,” The War Zone, December 13, 2024)

December 7 — 8:39 p.m. A United Airlines pilot flying over Willamette National Forest east of Eugene, Oregon, reports red, circular lights moving erratically toward the ocean and returning at various altitudes from 30,000 to 50,000 feet. Another crew member on the same flight observes the objects moving in corkscrew patterns at an extreme speed. At 8:46 p.m., a pilot flying a Life Flight medical evaluation plane over Siuslaw National Forest northwest of Eugene sees a red light going in circles about 20 miles away at an altitude of 1,000 feet. It zips toward the plane and then reverses to the ocean at high speed. A 44-minute recording of air traffic controllers talking to the pilots is archived from LiveATC.net. (“ Pilots Report Mysterious Lights ‘Moving at Extreme Speeds’ across Oregon Skies,” KGW-TV, Portland, Oreg., December 11, 2024; Flynn Nicholls, “ Pilots Told to ‘Maneuver; around Oregon ‘UFO’ in Leaked Cabin Audio,” Newsweek, December 11, 2024; Flynn Nicholls,“ Pilot Encountered Mystery Objects ‘Moving at Extreme Speed’: FAA,” Newsweek, December 12, 2024)

December 12 — 5:25 p.m. A witness in Clinton, New Jersey, watches a drone flying from northeast to north, dipping up and down while spraying a gray mist. The Transportation Security Administration identifies the object “with a high confidence level” as a Beechcraft Baron 58 aircraft experiencing turbulence. The gray mist is explained as a condensation cloud caused by rapid pressure changes over the surfaces of its wings. (Transportation Security Administration, “ LE/FAMS NWK Sightings Review,” December 17, 2024)

December 23 — Night. A flight crew is flying an empty private jet over the Bahamas when air traffic control in Miami, Florida, asks the pilot to identify an unknown radar target to the west. The pilot sees three objects, but flight attendant Cassandra Martin only sees one white light that turns slightly green. Martin takes a cellphone video that shows a spherical object darting about. It stays with the aircraft for 45 minutes before the crew loses sight of it. Later, they notice it has moved high above their altitude of 45,000 feet. (“ UFO Sighting? Fort Lauderdale Flight Crew Spots Something Strange in the Sky,” WTVJ-TV, Miami, Florida, January 9, 2025)

2025

January 3–4 — 10:30 p.m. From 4–20 mystery drones are reported above the marina at Køge, Denmark. Danish police verify the initial report, and the last drones are seen disappearing above the Køge Bugt at 1:16 a.m. (“ Mystiske dromer: Nu reagerer PET,” Ekstra Bladet (Copenhagen, Denmark), January 4, 2025; “ Danish Police Investigate Mystery Drone Sightings,” Deutsche Welle, January 4, 2025)

January 15 — The Office of the Chief Science Advisor of Canada releases its first preliminary report on the Management of Public Reporting of Unidentified Aerial Phenomena in Canada: A Preview of the Upcoming Sky Canada Report. It contains a Message from the chief science advisor, Mona Nemer, and an executive summary. These are followed by two appendices, the first a list of contributors and experts consulted and the second the results of a survey of Canadians by an outside agency regarding opinions on UAP. It recommends that a federal agency such as the Canadian Space Agency be designated to handle UAP reports, and that Transport Canada should actively encourage pilots to report UAP. A full report will be released later in the year. (Government of Canada, Preview: Sky Canada Report from the Office of the Chief Science Advisor of Canada, January 2025; Chris Rutkowski, “ The Sky Canada Project ‘Preview Report,’” Ufology Research, January 15, 2025; “ What We Learned from Canada’s First UFO Report in Decades,” CTV News, January 15, 2025; Baptiste Friscourt, “ Government: 27% of the Canadian Population Claim to Have Observed UFOs,” Sentinel News, February 18, 2025)

January 21 — 5:00 a.m. A witness near Hopwood, Pennsylvania, notices a light outside his window that is coming from three spherical objects, each the size of a basketball, sitting in his yard. They immediately come together to form a single white light that is much brighter and shoots up into the sky after a few seconds. (Stan Gordon, “ Three Glowing Orbs on the Ground Rise Straight Up into the Sky in Pennsylvania,” Stan Gordon’s UFO Anomalies Zone, February 1, 2025)

January 22 — Projekt Záře in the Czech Republic reports 41 observations of UFOs during 2024. (Martin Chlebovský, “ 2024 UAP Reports from Czechia,” UAP Check, January 22, 2025)

January 26 — 7:20 p.m. Two witnesses in Steeleville, Illinois, watch a silent object shaped like a black diamond moving to the northwest about 20 mph some 80 feet above their house. It has dimly glowing lights on its bottom front section. It remains in sight for 10 seconds. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting,” January 31, 2025)

February — Morning. Roughly 15 miles from Fort Worth, Texas, the pilot of a cargo aircraft encounters a white, elongated drone that passes approximately 100 feet above the cockpit while the plane is flying at 15,500 feet. “It appeared to be not a small hobby drone, and it looked maybe 3 to 4 feet long,” the pilot wrote in an Aviation Safety Reporting System report. (Tim McMillan, “‘ We Are Going to Have a Catastrophic Incident’: Drone Incursions in Restricted Airspace Are Surging in 2025,” The Debrief, May 30, 2025)

March 1 — Near Gillespie Field in El Cajon, California, the pilot of a Cessna 172 is forced to take evasive action to avoid a potential midair collision with a drone. Tower personnel confirms the UAV is flying at 1,000 feet, approximately half a mile west of the airport. The drone begins trailing the Cessna, prompting authorities to suspend all air operations at Gillespie for more than 30 minutes. A San Diego County Sheriff’s Department helicopter is dispatched to investigate, but deputies cannot locate the drone. (Tim McMillan, “‘ We Are Going to Have a Catastrophic Incident’: Drone Incursions in Restricted Airspace Are Surging in 2025,” The Debrief, May 30, 2025)

March 28 — The Japanese government’s UAP investigatory group holds a second general meeting that features online video presentations by Christopher Mellon, Timothy Gallaudet, Peter Skafish, and Rep. Eric Burlison. ([ The 2nd General Meeting of the Parliamentary League for Clarifying Unidentified Anomalous Phenomena from a National Security Perspective], Niconico News YouTube channel, March 27, 2025; Keith Basterfield, “ Recent Japanese Government Interest in UAP,” Unidentified Anomalous Phenomena—Scientific Research, March 31, 2025)

April 4 — Chris Rutkowski releases statistics on UFO reports in Canada during 2024, showing 1,008 reports filed, 3.77% of which are considered unexplained. (Chris Rutkowski, “ Results of the 2024 Canadian UFO Survey,” April 4, 2025)

April 24 — 9:00 p.m. Two witnesses observe a dark metallic, octahedron-shaped object near Granite High School in Porterville, California. The object, estimated to be 600–800 feet away and about the size of a UPS truck, flies silently and without lights, matching the vehicle’s speed (30–35 mph) while traveling parallel to it. When one of the witnesses points it out, the object instantly makes a sharp 90° turn and flies toward the city, disappearing after 10–15 seconds. The witness describes the craft as having markings or engravings—possibly resembling ancient hieroglyphics—visible due to moonlight. There are no windows, cockpit, or sound. (National UFO Reporting Center, “ NUFORC UFO Sighting 188813,” April 10, 2025)

May 16 — Members of the Japanese “Parliamentary League for UAP Clarification from a Security Perspective” deliver a formal proposal to Defense Minister Gen Nakatani, urging the government to strengthen surveillance and data collection in response to recent incursions by drones and surveillance balloons, particularly those believed to originate from China. The proposal calls for the ministry to form a specialized division focused on three key tasks: collecting and analyzing UAP-related data, disclosing relevant findings to the public, and reporting investigation results regularly to the National Diet. ([ The Bipartisan UAP Diet Members’ League], Fuji News Network, May 16, 2025)

June 16 — The Brazilian Air Force releases documents on 26 UFO sightings by military personnel in 2024. In two incidents, the UFOs disrupted the aircraft’s on-board electronics so that their position was visible on the collision avoidance system, even though they did not appear on the air traffic control radar. (Andrea Müller, “ Brasiliens Luftwaffe veröffentlicht UFO-Sichtungen durch Piloten 2024,” grenzWissenschaft- aktuell.de, June 16, 2025)

July 14 — Mona Nemer, Canada’s Chief Science Advisor, releases the final report of the Sky Canada Project, recommending the creation of a new federal body to standardize, collect, and investigate UFO sightings. The report specifically points to the Canadian Space Agency as a “trusted” scientific organization that could lead this new effort in collaboration with government and academic partners. It also recommends that Canadian aviation officials should do more when flight crews file UAP reports. Other recommendations include combatting disinformation, making UAP records available to the public, and creating tools for data collection. The report flags several government departments and agencies that routinely receive UAP reports, including Transport Canada, the Department of National Defence, the Canadian Space Agency, and the Royal Canadian Mounted Police. (Office of the Chief Science Advisor of Canada, Management of Public Reporting of Unidentified Aerial Phenomena in Canada, June 14, 2025; Daniel Otis, “ Canada’s Top Scientist Releases New UFO Report: Here’s What You Need to Know,” CTV News, July 14, 2025)

July 17 — 2:30–3:00 p.m. A woman is walking to her backyard garden near Monaca, Pennsylvania, when she sees a glowing white sphere about the size of a basketball about 5 feet above her sidewalk and blocking her way. It begins moving slowly toward her, stopping about 2 inches away. Then it moves closer and touches her. It seems to be metallic, but not stiff, and a bit cold. When it begins to push, she backs away, stumbles, and falls backward on the ground. The sphere hovers above her for a couple seconds, then vanishes. (Stan Gordon, “ Daylight Luminous Orb Approaches Witness and Makes Physical Contact in Pennsylvania,” Stan Gordon’s UFO Anomalies Zone, July 27, 2025)

Late July — Night. Four security guards near the main entrance to the Kyushu Electric Power Company’s Genkai Nuclear Power Station in Genkai, Saga Prefecture, Japan, see three drone-like lights. (“ Defense Experts, Lawmakers call for More Serious UFO Research,” Asahi Shimbun (Tokyo), September 4, 2025)

August 7 — Yasukazu Hamada and other members of the “Parliamentary League for UAP Clarification from a Security Perspective” in the House of Representatives of Japan’s National Diet hold closed- door hearings in the basement floor of the lower house’s office building to discuss the Genkai incident in July and other drone activity in Japan. Officials from the Nuclear Regulation Authority, the Defense Ministry, and the Land Ministry provide testimony. (“ Defense Experts, Lawmakers call for More Serious UFO Research,” Asahi Shimbun (Tokyo), eptember 4, 2025)

September 10 — MUFON releases statistics on UFO sightings reported to the organization in the first seven months of 2025. (Rob Swiatek, “ MUFON CMS Statistics for 2025: The First Seven Months,” Mutual UFO Network, September 10, 2025)
